# Text Elements
Step 2: Find the number of valence electrons ^RsXBIJfd

Step 3: Find the number of bonding electrons pairs ^nyThIEIr

Step 4: Find the number of lone electron pairs orbiting the central atom ^BhaoJ32G

Step 5: Work out the shape of the molecule based on the formula sheet ^ASOXMGSz
